create database workshop

create table coach
(	
	coachID			int			not null,
	coachForeName	varchar(20)	not null,
	coachSurName	varchar(20)	not null

	CONSTRAINT PKCoachID PRIMARY KEY (coachID)
)

create table workshops
(
	workshopID		int				not null,
	workshopName	varchar(100)	not null

	CONSTRAINT PKWorkshopID PRIMARY KEY (workshopID)
)

create table campus
(
	campusID		int				not null,
	campusName		varchar(100)	not null,	
	CONSTRAINT PKCampusID PRIMARY KEY (campusID)
)

create table course
(
	courseID		int				not null,
	courseName		varchar(200)	not null,
	courseSessName		varchar(200)		not null
	CONSTRAINT PKCourseID PRIMARY KEY (courseID)
)

create table session
(
	sessionID		int		not null,
	coachID			int		not null,
	workshopID		int		not null,
	campusID		int		not null,
	courseID		int		not null,
	courseDate		DATE	not null,
	courseTime		TIME	not null

	CONSTRAINT PKSessionID PRIMARY KEY (sessionID),
	CONSTRAINT FKCoachID FOREIGN KEY (coachID) REFERENCES coach(coachID),
	CONSTRAINT FKWorkshopID FOREIGN KEY (workshopID) REFERENCES workshops(workshopID),
	CONSTRAINT FKCampusID FOREIGN KEY (campusID) REFERENCES campus(campusID),
	CONSTRAINT FKCourseID FOREIGN KEY (courseID) REFERENCES course(courseID)
)

create table attendees(

	studentId	INT		NOT NULL,
	name	varchar(100)	not null,
	email	varchar(100)	not null,

	Constraint PKStudentID primary key (studentID)
)

create table sessionDetails(
	
	sessionID	int		not null,
	studentId	int		not null,

	constraint FKsessionID foreign key (sessionID) references session (sessionID),
	constraint FKstudentID foreign key (studentId) references attendees (studentId)
	constraint PKsessionStudent Primary key (sessionID, studentId)
)
